        <div class="cell destinationreview"></div>                    <div id="parent2325041" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.77);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:1,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="1"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2325041" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="danygurl06"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1204896"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1204896.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="danygurl06" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Dior/J-adore-Parfum-d-Eau-75642.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.75642.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="J'adore Parfum d'Eau"title="J'adore Parfum d'Eau"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2325041ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2325041" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.77); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1204896">danygurl06</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-23"></span><fromunixtime unixtime="1729704314" class="vote-button-legend"></fromunixtime></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I try not to give very negative reviews, but this stuff stinks so badly to me. There are notes in this fragrance that I obviously can't smell because all of the supposed inspired by/ similar fragrances smell nothing like it. They all smell sweet.  This smells like burnt rubber, latex, and Band-Aids. I get absolutely no sweetness. <br />
<br />
Too many have caught on to this perfume. I've even smelled it on Hospital patient transporters while already feeling sick.  Its so loud, sharp and headache inducing. It leaves such a long lasting scent trail. I think my dad's nose is similar to mine. He smelled someone wear it and after they left he negatively questioned what they wore.<br />
<br />
This isn't the only fragrance that smells awful to me. There are other fragrances ( that I don't know the name of) that typically older women wear that has the scent of straight up cat piss. No one else seems to smell that funk but me. I wish I could enjoy Baccarat Rouge 540 on myself or others. So many people are wearing it nowadays. I usually confirm with the wearer if its is BR 540 when I smell it on others and it always is. So this fragrance is very distinct.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="33519"comment_id="2325041"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Francis-Kurkdjian/Baccarat-Rouge-540-33519.html?ccid=2325041#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2322880" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.8);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:2,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Like people have said below, it's gives very old lady type vibes. Don't think it's bad but not sure if I would wear it myself. Biggest issue is really the price. There is no way it's worth the money it's been advertised. Or rather...I don't understand why EVERYONE wears it! All the cool kids and celebs think it's so unique but, um, they just smell like everyone else. So basic.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="33519"comment_id="2315958"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Francis-Kurkdjian/Baccarat-Rouge-540-33519.html?ccid=2315958#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2315792" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.81);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Its truly like no other fragrance I've smelt. If you are after an experience, and not a smell, this is the one for you. The scent opens very metallic and turns into this dance of sugary candied notes that spin around you playing hide and seek with your nose.<br />
The bad:<br />
It costs 300 dollars. I justify this price as part of the experience in that you will cherish it far more, but if you cannot stomach the price then I would say there are far too many similar options for pennies on the dollar to make a good argument for the original. Also, the fragrance is very linear and very divisive. Some smell latex gloves or hospital bandaids, while other smell heaven in a bottle.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="33519"comment_id="2315404"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Francis-Kurkdjian/Baccarat-Rouge-540-33519.html?ccid=2315404#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2315190" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.77);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />
My northern self wanted to see what a bit of London smelt like. And if that’s what it smells like then I’ll stay up here with the flowers, fields and farm animals. <br />
<br />
This is not an offensive scent but it’s just lacklustre, dull and overhyped. It’s a woody amber (my nose smells amber the most), with not much depth or development. <br />
<br />
It does give a good scent radius and it lasts a good amount of time. It’s just….nothing special. <br />
<br />

Unfortunately on me it does project as strong, however definitely a nice clean floral scent that’s not overly feminine . A mass appealing scent that’ll definitely get compliments. Wish I got more wood notes but overall special. If you’re looking for something unique this isn’t for you, if you’re looking for a safe niche blind buy, this is for you.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="33519"comment_id="2294602"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Francis-Kurkdjian/Baccarat-Rouge-540-33519.html?ccid=2294602#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2294192" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.82);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:1,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2274324" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="elijah.rb71"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2238515"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2238515.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="elijah.rb71" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2274324ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck2x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2274324" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.85); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2238515">elijah.rb71</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-07">09/07/24 01:21</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I think most people have tried Baccarat by now, and I can see why it is so popular, but it really was not a favorite of mine. To me, this has a very metallic/damp smell to it. It's almost like the notes are all there but covered in some sort of ever-present metallic note that I just can't seem to shake. Weirdly enough, I like the smell of it on others, but I just cannot stand it on myself. With that being said, it is a very universal scent, as I feel like it would really blend in with any time of the day/time of the year.<br />
<br />
The performance is also great. I got pretty long stretches of good performance out of it, usually about 8-10 hours depending on the day, with pretty fantastic sillage to boot. I also really like how unisex this scent is. Despite it's at times overwhelming sweetness, it is really truly a scent to be worn by anyone which is always nice. I do also feel like the price tag should be a point of discussion, as it is pretty pricey. Not exactly Tom Ford pricey (though this would certainly be more worth that price point than some TF fragrances) but not cheap either. Overall, I do think everyone should give this now iconic fragrance a go at some point, but it really isn't for me. I still love the way it smells on others though!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="33519"comment_id="2274324"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Francis-Kurkdjian/Baccarat-Rouge-540-33519.html?ccid=2274324#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2273256" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.78);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Utopian, sterile, and perfectly in control with an underlying rage. I imagine this is the signature scent of Joe from You, Dexter Morgan, Norman Bates, and Hannibal Lecter. Did I mention this smells like latex?</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="33519"comment_id="2267447"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Francis-Kurkdjian/Baccarat-Rouge-540-33519.html?ccid=2267447#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2266873" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.9);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:1,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="1"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2052153">aininia</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-08-27">08/27/24 01:56</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Baccarat Rouge 540 is literally the scent of a butterfly that I’m trying to catch. I’m definitely late to the party, and I blame all the dupes for that. After only smelling the replicas, I wasn’t that curious about the original, but I’m glad to say I was wrong.<br />
<br />
Baccarat Rouge is a magical fragrance. I find the notes hard to grasp and hold onto. It has a freshness, but I can also sense the burnt sugar, yet it’s not exactly sweet. There’s something glossy and cool about it, but it still feels warm. Metallic, sweet, ethereal, supernatural, and elegant. If Ambrosia, the food of the gods, had a scent.<br />
<br />
The blend is so soft, smooth, and ethereal that it’s almost impossible to dissect, and I love that. It’s like those things you reluctantly become addicted to—it sticks with you, and you want to experience it again and again, a bit like a childhood crush.<br />
<br />
There are fragrances I like more, but BR540 is still a clear 10/10—an obsession, a timeless classic and legend that I deeply cherish.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2172275">Nadya2024</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-08-22">08/22/24 10:40</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I heard a lot about this perfume, and when started journey to niche perfumes world, decided to try it out. Even purchasing a sample is not cheap, but I had to. When I sprayed a fist time, I thought it was a joke. I didn’t like it at all. As it set on my skin, one minute I would hate it, another wonder if there is something in it that I liked. <br />
<br />
I walked into the room where my husband was sitting (and he does not like most of the perfumes probably lol) he asked me what perfume I was wearing. Then he  said best perfume ever, buy a full bottle. I laughed and said, do you know how much it cost. He said figure out how to save money and  buy it.<br />
<br />
 I was puzzled, and next few days kept on playing with the scent. Each time I was realizing more and more, I was falling for this perfume. Two weeks later, I had to buy full bottle. Ever since, it was one of my favorite perfumes. I tried all sort of dupes for it, but nothing compares to original for me. The others might smell kind of close in smell, but none of them carry this light vail that surrounds you. Sometime you think smell is gone, and then you catch smell lightly hugging you. It can be smelled the moment myself or someone approach the crowd. But it never becomes overpowering or heavy. <br />
<br />
I think it is definitely one of controversial perfumes. Either you love it, or don’t. But now I think it is true masterpiece and would be in my collection for long long time.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="33519"comment_id="2257430"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Francis-Kurkdjian/Baccarat-Rouge-540-33519.html?ccid=2257430#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2256245" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.82);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1658856">darlindearest</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-08-21">08/21/24 09:17</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>It’s actually insane how late I am to the baccarat obsession party. But here I am and oh my god I’m here to stay. I took a little bit of a roundabout to get to baccarat itself and began my acquaintance with it through Burberry Her. I liked the juiciness and loudness of Her and thought well if it’s a dupe and I’m into it let’s do it. I was also aware that baccarat is kind of divisive: it smells medicinal to some while others say it’s burnt sugar type of sweet. Well, even if it goes medicinal on me, I reasoned, I have gucci memoire d’une and it’s kind of medicinal and I love it. Upon the first spray I was underwhelmed, I don’t even remember what it smelled like to me at that moment but I was like, eh? Then it sat on my arm for a couple of minutes and it did turn sort of medicinal but I was into it. The next day I actually wore it and what a 360 it did on me, gone was the medicine cabinet which was replaced by syrupy sweetness akin to Her and I still loved it. A couple of wears in and baccarat smells like burnt sugar, sweet ,rich and I don’t know how it works but so confidence boosting. Later on I also decided to try Cloud and well, both Cloud and Her are good dupes (Her is a little bit better of the two imo ; probably because it’s Kurkdjian who made it as well) but they kind of lack the backbone, they are airier (especially Cloud) and dare I say less luxurious. I’ve only worn baccarat in the summer so far and I cannot wait to try it in colder weather. Also I go partially anosmic to it but I catch whiffs of it off of myself well into 6-9 hours of wearing it.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="33519"comment_id="2256245"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Francis-Kurkdjian/Baccarat-Rouge-540-33519.html?ccid=2256245#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2255387" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.84);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; 15:46</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>MFK BR 540 is an Ok fragrance if you're familiar with middle eastern fragrances , its very similar to that region creations but its westernized and by that i mean its softer , rounder!! and without any funky notes (like earthiness or dirtiness) but still has a pleasant darkness , upon spraying you are welcomed by the sweet and slightly spicy aroma of the red gold (that's another name for saffron in ME) with an underlying woody note this part is warm , sweet , slightly spicy as mentioned and slightly sued like , this is what most people call Amber aroma (fun fact : there is nothing as Amber in the world but the fantasy aroma accord is created by combining notes such as saffron , sandalwood , labdanum , iso E , benzoin , some musks or ... the combination and amount used ,is unique to perfumer so, amber notes are somewhat different in any perfume) after the initial aroma settles there will be a dark green, slightly fresh, woody ,slightly salty note adds to the mix makes the experience slightly more interesting , i initially thought that , this contains vetiver but that isn't mentioned anywhere  🤷 any ways after a certain time period the perfume settles to a soft , slightly sweet and woody note with a bit of darkness and bite (almost like an oud note) , this part is also very pleasant and it stays for sometime like this before it fades , overall very good and professionally made but still , its an Ok one nothing to boast or groundbreaking  specially at this price! for instance Raghba by Lattaffa also an OK perfume , wanders in the same waters as BR 540 but Raghba is rougher around the edges , its darker ,earthy-er and a bit smokier and not as well made but if one fancies such smells, one can try it for cheap , at last this smells better and sexier on a Lady than a Bloke 😉😎 👌</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div It's the cedar.<br />
<br />
Late review here. Burnt sugar almost with the smell of... new car? (I purchased the body oil). Poor description, I know.. but it's sultry and intriguing. Longevity and sillage is ok on me. I wear it over a neutral lotion. In my opinion, the hype is 100% worth it. I hope they never discontinue or reformulate this one. I can see it being known as the Chanel of our generation down the line (given that almost every woman including myself owns this or a dupe of it). I also sampled a couple of other scents from this house - absolutely fantastic.<br />
<br />
For everyone saying it's too popular just remember that you bring the personality to a perfume, not the other way around. Ergo, everyone will present something different when they wear it. AND add to it that everyone's skin chemistry will also present this different.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="33519"comment_id="2237327"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Francis-Kurkdjian/Baccarat-Rouge-540-33519.html?ccid=2237327#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2237229" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.73);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2107198">venussiandehermes</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-07-31">07/31/24 15:38</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This fragrance is truly a masterpiece of perfumery. People are serious polarizers in terms of their tastes. Whenever I wear this fragrance, my mother says that the scent gives her a headache, but I can't help but smell my arm every few minutes. This scent really draws me in. <br />
<br />
A very refined amber scent. It seems like there are shadows in the scent's profile. These shadows consist of some layers. The feeling that the scent leaves in the nose during a breath has shaded transitions from the beginning to the end of the breath. The amber here changes in a few seconds from a dark sugary red syrup atmosphere to released into a woody and leathery layer. Probably the use of saffron note reminds me of the feeling of leather. I experience this oscillation in the scent every time I smell it. <br />
<br />
This fragrance is not my favorite, but it is one of the ones that surprised and amazed me the most. Even though it is very popular, do not think that it is a perfume that is popular with everyone. Even the polarizing profile of this perfume is enough to show that it is an icon of modern perfumery.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="33519"comment_id="2235009"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Francis-Kurkdjian/Baccarat-Rouge-540-33519.html?ccid=2235009#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2234222" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.74);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1043744">FreshLiving</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-07-21">07/21/24 19:18</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Finally have gotten around to trying this after reading about it for years. And after trying it, I have smelt this many times before in my life in various environments. I just didn’t know it was this. So I can see how this fragrance is continually talked about and continues to inspire. <br />
<br />
Have this on my hand now; sprayed it 5 hours ago.<br />
The initial blast and first two hours are sweet, a bit too much for my taste. But the aroma is very pleasing. Upon dry down while the sweetness recedes after 3 hours it’s just an incredible scent. I wish it opened up less sweet and was the way it is on dry down. Now it is a very nice woody, spicy, oceanic like refreshing bubble on my hand that’s wafts up to intoxication.<br />
<br />
I have ordered a 1ml sample, and when it arrives I’ll try it over the course of a week and see my final verdict. <br />
I currently have a fragrance card of it and often find myself smelling it due to how intoxicating the scent is.<br />
<br />
**EDIT**<br />
Upon more wearing and after sampling the extrait version, I can’t stop having the scent and association that many have mentioned in the extract version. That this smells a bit dental or like fluoride. It seems it’s all I can smell now when I use my sample. I get whiffs of my earlier write up but now I do get too much of that latex glove scent. <br />
I may have to let this fish go for someone else to catch.<br />
MFK is a great house though.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="33519"comment_id="2225617"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Francis-Kurkdjian/Baccarat-Rouge-540-33519.html?ccid=2225617#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2223573" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.89);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; If NYC was a perfume, this would be it. It’s sweet, salty, bright, light but deep, complex, ambroxan, airy and interesting. I love smelling it on my skin— it makes me feel like I’m sparkling and lasts so long, I wake up with jammy, sweet amber-y notes that I love. However, it gives me a headache when I smell it on passer-bys in hot summer weather and makes me slightly annoyed because it is EVERYWHERE in NYC. I can’t help but wonder if other people feel the same when I put it on too :/ It feels suffocating in hot weather and icy in cold weather. I think fall and spring are perfect for it. Some days I love it more than any other perfume, others I dislike it and find it over-done. In many ways, it reminds me of the love-hate relationship I have with NYC. I would buy it if it was like 40 dollars</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="33519"comment_id="2209781"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Francis-Kurkdjian/Baccarat-Rouge-540-33519.html?ccid=2209781#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2209120" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.73);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1445544">jbozz</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-07-05">07/05/24 10:54</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Overhyped, overreviewed, overcloned, overdone, overworn, you can say whatever you want to say about Baccarat Rouge 540, because in 2024 this stuff is still beautiful and nothing out there matches the quality of the original. I do get just a bit of that “latex glove” note in the opening, but that lasts all of maybe 2-3 minutes for me. Once it starts to dry down it’s just that sexy, slightly burnt cotton candy vibe, and how he managed to make this to be sweet yet light and airy all at once is nothing short of brilliant; and yes this still pulls compliments better than most. BR540 is right up there with the likes of Aventus, Santal 33, Layton, and could arguably be the best of the lot. A masterpiece fragrance in any case.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="33519"comment_id="2209120"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Francis-Kurkdjian/Baccarat-Rouge-540-33519.html?ccid=2209120#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2207973" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.73);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2202038" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Lady Nightshadow"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1218445"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1218445.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Lady Nightshadow" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2202038ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck6x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2202038" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.89); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1218445">Lady Nightshadow</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-06-28">06/28/24 09:05</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I've tested Baccarat two times in the last month, from different boutiques, just to have a clue about this alleged masterpiece. <br />
<br />
To my surprise, the blend of spices and resin of Baccarat comes across as sticky sweet.<br />
I smell a cherry syrup which is nowhere to be found in pyramid but, to me, is the absolute main character of this fragrance.<br />
While I love sweet vanilla fragrances, this has more of a sugar candy vibe.<br />
<br />
I was expecting something much deeper, more prominent woods, but still, this is a very "adult woman" scent, extremely warm and well blended.<br />
<br />
The fruity sweet note doesn't come across as childish since there's something resinous in here that remotely reminds me of Alien. <br />
They're completely different, but both share an odd balsamic note, which is much lighter and blended here in Baccarat.<br />
<br />
Overall, it's a pleasant fragrance, one that I've already smelled on women aged 45+.<br />
It gives a wealthy old money, put together vibe.<br />
Not my cup of tea, but it's a thumb up nonetheless.<br />
<br />
An opinion nobody asked for: <br />
<br />
I'd like to see more respect for the people that work behind fragrances and for those who love a scent even when we don't like it.<br />
Belittling them and mocking them for whatever reason is bully behavior. <br />
Disappointment can be expressed in many ways, even harsh ones, without being rude.<br />
<br />
The undeniable success of Baccarat just can't be reduced to a matter of fashion trends. <br />
<br />
Since Baccarat is still going strong years after its release, which is not easy for this price point to begin with, it's obvious that the nose who worked on it did something right.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; At first sniff it was so polarizing.. so different from anything I had ever smelled before. I was confused by what I was smelling simply bc I didn't know how to describe it. I don't think there is very much middle ground with br540.. you either love it or you don't like it at all. Before I smelled this fragrance I never thought of perfumery as an art form. This fragrance made me look at perfumery differently. I came to the conclusion that anyone who could take the notes in that scent pyramid and make it smell like what was in that bottle is a master of his craft. I truly feel like this fragrance is a masterpiece. It's still hard for me to describe it. To my nose it is ambery cotton candy heaven. It is a scent profile that I will forever love. I love the way it makes me feel when I wear it. I feel like I can't lose. Love it or hate it... It is definitely one of the most polarizing scents ever.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="33519"comment_id="2200171"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Francis-Kurkdjian/Baccarat-Rouge-540-33519.html?ccid=2200171#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2200133" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.86);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:1,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2171368">vk0</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-06-26">06/26/24 11:16</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Bahrain Airport 26.06.2024<br />
Light at first smell, but more than 4 sprays can feel quite overwhelming for a few seconds; it made my head feel full despite being so light. After a few minutes though, it leaves only a very light trace on the skin and has a much lower sillage than other perfumes I’ve had (though I haven’t asked anyone else if they can smell it on me or not). I can’t seem to catch the definitive scent of it just a few minutes after spraying it, but I am aware of its presence. The scent I got on the first spritz seems to dart around every time I smell my wrists or clothes, always giving me most of the notes but never all of them. The pieces I do get are quite pleasant, though I can't seem to shake off the feeling of some form of cleaning product or alcohol from it. I initially had it on my to-get list (albeit quite low down) just after the first smell, however after listening to the advice of Scout Dixon West (though anyone else would have said to do this) and letting it settle on my skin, I’ve realised in less than 15 minutes that it might not be for me. However, it could just be that it’s an old airport tester as the ones next to Baccarat Rouge were running out, so I’ll have to try it again. <br />
As for the bottle, as with all MFK fragrances I have seen (this has always been in perfume stores), it feels wonderful to hold and looks very elegant too.<br />
This isn't meant to be a review, just a personal record</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="33519"comment_id="2200133"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Francis-Kurkdjian/Baccarat-Rouge-540-33519.html?ccid=2200133#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2199785" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.84);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; In conclusion, this shit is not worth the price at all, it's just bad, that's all that can really be said.<br />

You can also pick it out of a line up. Every. Single. Time. If someone’s wearing Baccarat, you will definitely know. <br />
<br />
The saffron, ambergris, and amberwood prominently stand out. <br />
<br />
This perfume has tons of depth. This perfume will guide you by the hand through the journey that is BR540. <br />
<br />
Wearing this is an experience. Some may like it, some may not. It is strong. It is potent. It is quite in your face. If you don’t enjoy nauseatingly striking fragrances, you probably may not like this, as it may give you a headache. Be aware not to overspray, you’ll regret it. <br />
<br />
This perfume smells like Fran from the Nanny. This is how I picture a woman that’s wearing BR540. She’s brunette with hair rollers, preparing for a night out at one of the most expensive casinos in town. She’s wearing a short, velvet black dress. She has a striking French red lip on. She’s wearing rubies. She may be wearing patent Lou Boutin platforms. She drives a black Maserati.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="33519"comment_id="2195042"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Francis-Kurkdjian/Baccarat-Rouge-540-33519.html?ccid=2195042#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2195009" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.7);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2172526">Emily_peterson1995</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-06-21">06/21/24 02:46</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Baccarat Rouge 540 is a masterpiece in the world of fragrances. Everytime I wear this perfume, I am instantly captivated by its luxurious and complex scent.<br />
<br />
The opening is a delightful blend of saffron and jasmine that feels both warm and inviting. As it develops, the heart of amberwood and ambergris brings a rich and slightly sweet complexity that is utterly enchanting. Finally, the base of fir resin and cedar adds a subtle, woody depth that lingers beautifully.<br />
<br />
One of the standout features of Baccarat Rouge 540 is its longevity. It lasts a remarkable 10-12 hours on my skin, with a sillage that draws compliments throughout the day. The fragrance is perfect for both special occasions and everyday wear, thanks to its versatile and sophisticated profile.<br />
<br />
Despite its premium price, the quality and experience of Baccarat Rouge 540 make it worth every penny. It’s a fragrance that truly stands out and leaves a lasting impression. Highly recommended for anyone looking to invest in a high-end, captivating scent!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="33519"comment_id="2194902"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Francis-Kurkdjian/Baccarat-Rouge-540-33519.html?ccid=2194902#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2194520" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.85);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1099233">Tyriel</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2018-10-09">10/09/18 00:05</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I smelled this fragrance at a person's place, who was shrinking his 500+ fragrance collection. I have smelled over 30 fragrances that afternoon and this is the only one that got stuck in my head. It has been over two months since I sniffed it and I cannot get it out of my head. I have never experienced this before. It is a strange experience. It's like I can smell it by just thinking about it. So I could not stop myself from buying a bottle.<br />
<br />
This fragrance is more than a scent. It is a scented journey. An olfactory wonder. A masterpiece. There is something about this scent, the way it smells, the way it performs. It is the most mysterious fragrance I own. When you spray it on, you smell it, but you kind of not smell it. However, even if you do not smell it, you know it is there. You sort of 'feel' its presence.<br />
<br />
I have not worn it in public yet, because it is quite a daring fragrance and a bit on the feminine side if you ask me.<br />
<br />
I bought a 200ml bottle and decided to decant 100ml of it, to pay off some of the mortgage I had to take to buy a bottle. The tube coming out of the bottle is not really suited to extract the juice with a syringe, so I taped-off a beaker and sprayed the juice until I got the required amount of juice needed for my decants (yes, my finger hurt afterwards). After filling the vials, I put the beaker in a room upstairs.The empty (yes, empty) beaker has been standing in this room for one week and the whole room has been smelling like Baccarat Rouge for one week. This is beyond beastmode.<br />
<br />
Scent: 11/10<br />
Projection: 11/10 (Projects very far for a good 4 hours and does not really come close to the skin for another 4 hours)<br />
Sillage: 10/10<br />
Longevity: 11/10 (14h+ on skin, days on clothes)<br />
Versatility 7/10 (Only for the coolest of days)<br />
Uniqueness: 9/10<br />
Price-performance: 9/10 (It is expensive, but beautiful and beastly)<br />
Total: 9.5</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="33519"comment_id="989504"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Francis-Kurkdjian/Baccarat-Rouge-540-33519.html?ccid=989504#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent896019" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.87);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1108402">NixNox</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2019-02-05">02/05/19 11:31</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I used to have a really good friend when I was a teenager - he used to go out with my sister when I was younger and after they broke up I remained friends with him. We used to sit around at his house down the road; swap books, listen to music. His Mum ran a beauticians from the house - it was a big house with an annex that she had converted into this beauty spa. She did facials, massages, aromatherapy and all that stuff for the local women. I always loved the scent of their house - like sweet berries mixed with chamomile, soft leather jackets and something antiseptic coming from the beautician's annex. It was comforting and captivating. It was such a strong and distinctive smell that all their family carried around on their clothes and bodies - I have often tried to find a scent that carries that smell. I haven't ever been able to find it.<br />
<br />
His Mother died of cancer at a relatively young age - not long after the time I used to go round almost every day. When I tried Baccarat Rouge 540 for the first time, it brought back the memory of his mother so strongly for me.  It doesn't smell exactly like the scent of their house - it is missing some aspect of the chamomile and leather I remember, though the saffron in Baccarat evokes that feel at a parallel - but it just took me straight back to that time. Something about the sweet scent of expensive oils and lotions mixed with the tang of antiseptic fluid she used to keep the room clean. I love this perfume - I think it's a true work of art to be capable of evoking such emotion in the wearer. I have many perfumes that I like very much and that give me great pleasure; very few of them make me feel something like this does.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; I envy those who get cotton candy, rich amber, and the gorgeous different experiences I've read in the reviews below. For me, I'll be sitting in the waiting room for my annual teeth cleaning.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="33519"comment_id="1300352"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Francis-Kurkdjian/Baccarat-Rouge-540-33519.html?ccid=1300352#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1535991" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.82);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1535991" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="bazbazar"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1398326"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1398326.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="bazbazar" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/DedCool/Fragrance-01-Taunt-52312.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.52312.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Fragrance 01 Taunt"title="Fragrance 01 Taunt"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1535991ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck9x1"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1535991" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.82); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1398326">bazbazar</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2022-04-03">04/03/22 10:00</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I was left so shaken by BR540. It has a nauseating iodine-like scent that lingers and even scrubbing does not help. I can concede and say that it does, indeed "smell rich", but not a delicate, comfortable "I live in the Ritz and vacation to Europe" way, rather in a scary, "generations of my family have owned mines all over the global south", "grandpa is on his seventh heart transplant surgery and grandma poisoned her servant" one. This fragrance scares me, i'm 100% serious. It evokes a visceral reaction, maybe it's the saffron... I really enjoyed the Extrait de Parfum however, it's a lot more comforting, sweeter even.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="33519"comment_id="1535991"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Francis-Kurkdjian/Baccarat-Rouge-540-33519.html?ccid=1535991#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1027144" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.89);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1027144" class="cell small-2" ><div ><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="modudupup"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1037723"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="modudupup" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Le-Labo/Iris-39-6336.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.6336.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Iris 39"title="Iris 39"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1027144ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck9x1"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1027144" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"><div class="flex-child-shrink" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.89); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1037723">modudupup</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2019-02-02">02/02/19 13:24</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This fragrance has everything I dislike in a perfume. Highly synthetic, cloyingly sweet, plastic opening. A strange, medicinal gauze and latex scent that as some say, reminds one of a hospital.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="33519"comment_id="1027144"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Francis-Kurkdjian/Baccarat-Rouge-540-33519.html?ccid=1027144#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1112257" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.71);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1112257" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Pandarapt"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1143418"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1143418.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Pandarapt" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Chanel/Chanel-No-5-Eau-de-Parfum-40069.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.40069.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Chanel No 5 Eau de Parfum"title="Chanel No 5 Eau de Parfum"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1112257ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck9x1"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1112257" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.71); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1143418">Pandarapt</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2019-11-03">11/03/19 12:13</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Hipsteria, Imma let you finish, but I personally don’t think Baccarat Rouge is the best fragrance of all time.  I don´t like doing negative reviews, especially since I consider  Kurkdijan one of the best perfumers today, so I’ll rip this one quick and easy like a bandaid. <br />
<br />
 To me it smells like the interior of my mom’s old medicine cabinet, an inorganic, synthetic sweetness reminding me of Merbromim solutions mixed with several cough syrups. Cold maltol sugars and antiseptic. It is underlined by a strange oceanic vibe and the image hammering my brain is of a sugar glass isomalt sculpture that someone dropped into a fish tank. <br />
<br />
Maybe my skin chemistry is thwarting the fragrance, who knows, but I’ll say this, there are times when you take away the weird medicine underbelly that the fragrance reminds me of red silk over a lighted lamp in a dark room, and the progression is like seeing the shadows of the surrounding objects billowing through its walls. And that part is rather beautiful.<br />
<br />
*This review is not intended as a criticism on anyone or their tastes, just my subjective interpretation of a smell and my silly take on it.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="33519"comment_id="1112257"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Francis-Kurkdjian/Baccarat-Rouge-540-33519.html?ccid=1112257#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div>                            <reviews-infinity :random-colors="[&quot;#fefcee&quot;,&quot;#faf7ec&quot;,&quot;#f9f9f3&quot;,&quot;#f8f9ec&quot;,&quot;#fffdea&quot;,&quot;#faf9fb&quot;,&quot;#faf5f2&quot;,&quot;#f7f4f2&quot;]" :perfume-id="33519" sentiment="negative"></reviews-infinity>
